 ori $29, $29, 2000

 jal init_patterns

;..........register test..........;
jal reset_offsets
register_operation:
 jal init_upward_1
 jal store_load_upward_0
 jal store_load_downward_1

jal reset_offsets
register_operation_2:
 jal init_upward_0
 jal store_load_upward_1
 jal store_load_downward_0

;........other test........;
;........reset $28 back for loops........;
 lui $28, 0
 ori $28, $28, 332

 lui $29, 1
 ori $29, $29, 2000

jal reset_offsets
operation_addu:
	jal load_patterns
	addu $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_addu

jal reset_offsets
operation_and:
	jal load_patterns
	and $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_and

jal reset_offsets
operation_nor:
	jal load_patterns
	nor $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_nor

jal reset_offsets
operation_or:
	jal load_patterns
	or $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_or

jal reset_offsets
operation_subu:
	jal load_patterns
	subu $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_subu

jal reset_offsets
operation_xor:
	jal load_patterns
	xor $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_xor

jal reset_offsets
operation_sllv:
	jal load_patterns
	sllv $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_sllv

jal reset_offsets
operation_slt:
	jal load_patterns
	slt $18, $2, $3
	sw $18, 0($29)
	jal increment_offset
	bne $27, $28, operation_slt
